 lekin system ke paas meraa biomitric he
 There are many misconceptions about Aadhaar
 iske sabase bade virdohi ve hai, jo soochna kaa adhikaar laae
 The poor have no objection

 Should we put an end to it? Not naturally
 niztaa bhrasht or aatankwaadiyon kaa kavach nahin ban sakati or use aisa bananaa bhi nahin chahie
 But authentically collected authentic people's data should not be transferred for unauthorized use and i am very clear about that
 maine jukerbarg ko bataaya ki narendra modi sarkaar press kii aazaadee, abhivyakti kii swatantraaa or soshal media main mukt vimarsh kii puri tarah se himachati he

 Section 43A also provides for compensation for not keeping data safe

 The government as an institution is accountable to the court for the protection of fundamental rights and the right to privacy is enshrined in Article 21

 *** dashahra yani vijaydashami hinduon kaa ek pramukh tyohaar he
 It is organized on the tenth day of the Shukla Paksha of Ashwin month
 bhagwaan ram ne isi din ravan kaa vadh kiya tha
 It is celebrated as the victory of truth over untruth
 isiliye is dashami ko vijayadashami ke naam se janaa jaataa he

 pracheen kaal main raja log is din vijay kii prarthana kar ran-yatra ke liye prasthaan karte the

 ramlila kaa aayojan hota he
 a huge effigy of Ravana is made and lit

 yah harsh or ullas tathaa vijay kaa parv he
 Dussehra is celebrated across the country on the occasion of Ramlila, which celebrates the victory of Lord Rama over Ravana, Dussehra symbolizes the victory of good over evil
 isse pehle navaratri ke dauraan anek sthanon par ramlilaayen yojit kii jaati he
 a huge effigy of Ravana, his brother Kumbhakarna and son Meghnad is burnt at many other places besides the Ramlila Maidan near the historic Red Fort in Delhi
 aisa karne kii peeche yah manyata he ki adharm par dharm kii or asaty par satya kii jeet hui he
 Thousands of people are present here on this day
 deshbhar main is din logon main utsaah dekhte hi banataa he
 With the passage of time, there has been a constant change in the way, their level and quality of presenting Ramlila
 ramlilaon kaa mordan hota swaroopaajkal ramlila manchan main modern takneekon kaa istemaal kiya ja rahaa he
 Many scenes of Ramleela are being presented through modern techniques and computers in such a way that they touch the reality
 lalakila kii lila main jahaan putalon kaa dahan electronic tareeke se hota he vahiin desh ke anya bhaagon main ramlila main computariced bhawan bhi dekhne ko milte hai

 samay ke saath kuch takneekon kaa prayog kar isse or zyada darshak ke jodne kaa prayaas kiya jaataa he
 What is the social significance of Dussehra? There is also the cultural aspect of Dussehra
 bharat krishi pradhan desh he
 When a farmer grows a golden crop in his field and brings home the wealth of grain, there is no limit to his euphoria and enthusiasm
 is prasannataa ke avasar par vah bhagwaan kii krupa ko maanata he or use prakat karne ke liye vah uskaa pujan karata he
 This festival is celebrated in different ways in different regions all over India
 maharashtra main is avasar par silangan ke naam se saamaajik mahotsav manaaya jaataa he
 In the evening, all the villagers come back to their village after looting the golden leaves of the Shami tree after crossing the border of the village, equipped with beautiful new clothes
 phir us swarna rupi patton kaa paraspar aadan-pradaan kiya jaataa he
 How to celebrate Dussehra in various regions of India? Whether Dussehra or Vijayadashami is celebrated as the victory of Rama or as Durga Puja, it is a festival of Shakti Puja in both the forms
 is din shastron kii puja bhi kii jaati he
 It is a festival of joy and joy and victory
 desh ke kone-kone main yah vibhinn roopon se manaaya jaataa he
 : -1
 himachal pradesh main kullu kaa dashahra bahut prasiddh he
 Like other places, the preparation of this festival starts ten days or a week in advance
 stri or purush sundar vastron se sajjit hokar turahi, bigul, dhol, nagaade, bansuri athwa jiske paas jo vaadya hota he, use lekar baahar nikalate hai
 The hill people worship their rural deity in a pompous procession
 devataaon kii murtiyon ko bahut hi aakarshak palki main sundar dhang se sajaayaa jaataa he
 Also they worship their main deity Raghunath ji
 is juluus main prashikshit nartak nati nrity karte hai
 In this way, they take a procession and revolve the city through the main parts of the city and begin the celebration of Dussehra in Kullu city with the worship of the deity Raghunathji
 dashami ke din is utsav kii shobhaa niraali hoti he

 purush aapas main gale milte hai

 In Tamil Nadu, Andhra Pradesh and Karnataka, Dussehra lasts for nine days in which three goddesses worship Lakshmi, Saraswati and Durga
 pehle teen din lakshmi, dhan or samruddhi kii devi, kaa pujan hota he

 pujan sthal ko acchhee tarah phulon or dipakon se sajaayaa jaataa he

 is samay prasiddh mysore mahal ko deepamalikaon se dulhan kii tarah sajaayaa jaataa he

 Information Commissioner Yashovardhan Azad gave this order on the application of RTI activist Nutan Thakur
 unhone mantralay se deshbhar main vibhinn ipies adhikariyon ke khilaaf darj aapraadhik maamalon kaa byoraa maanga tha
 In its reply, the Police Branch of the Ministry of Home Affairs has said that the Police-1 Division of the Ministry does not keep files regarding criminal cases filed against IPS officers
 aaazaad ne kaha, ‘‘piaio ne kaha ki chunki grih mantralay kaa police divijan ipies adhikariyon ke khilaaf darj aapraadhik maamalon kaa is tarah kaa byoraa nahin rakhata he, isliye sawaal ko rashtriya aparaadh record beuro ko sthanantarit kar diya gaya
 The PIO expressed ignorance when the commission asked for the reason for transfer of the RTI application
 ’’ Azad noted that the RTI application was transferred without using discretion
 unhone kaha, ‘‘enciarabi bade paimaane par aparaadh ke aankade rakhata he or vah apilkarta kii jaruraton ke hisaab se aankadon ko alag karke nahin rakhata he
 Azad said that the Ministry of Home Affairs, being the parent ministry of the IPS cadre, always receives information when a charge sheet is filed against an officer
 deshbhar main grih mantralay ke tahat takreeban 9000 adhikari hai
 Azad is a former IPS officer who served as a senior officer in the intelligence system before joining the CIC
 unhone kaha, ‘‘adhikari kaa rajya cader aavantit kiye jane ke baavjood nodel agency hone ke naate grih mantralay ke paas sevarat ipies adhikariyon ke khilaaf darj maamalon kaa byoraa avashya hona chahie
 However, according to the PIO, there is no list of names of IPS officers against whom criminal cases have been filed
 ’’ Azad asked the ministry official to give an affidavit regarding the statement that there was no list of IPS officers facing criminal cases
 unhone kaha, ‘‘cader niyantrak praadhikaar hone ke naate grih mantralay kii bhoomika ipies adhikariyon kii seva sharton ko dekhne kii he
 Disciplinary proceedings are part of that role as it is kept in the private files of the officers
 ’’tippaniyan The information commissioner said that the work of the ministry is also to supervise disciplinary proceedings and investigate against the officials
 impanelament kii prakriya ke dauraan iskaa vishleshan kiya jaataa he

 sies : agar apane saath har jagah laptop le janaa he to 13 se14 inch vaale laptop aapke liye besthai

 oparating system:appal ke fain hai ? mike oes pasand he ? agar haa to aapke liye limited opshans hai
 If you want a Windows based laptop, you have a lot of options
 hardware spacification:heavi yuj he or bajet bhi thik thaak he to spacifications ke saath koi samjhauta na karen
 Take a laptop with at least 4GB of RAM, no less
 hard discs:1tibi hard discs honi chahie orprocesar speed bhi tejaho
 If you have the option of SSD in hard disk, then buy it only because it will be very fast
 haalanki iske liye aapako zyada paise dene honge

 kuch laptops ke procesar speed compair kar len to or bhi acha hoga

 saadhaaran yuj ke liye echdi screen (1366 x 768) hai

 The Hague-based International Court of Justice (ICJ) has asked India to complete arguments in the Kulbhushan Jadhav case by 13 September
 videsh mantralay ne shuukravaar ko yah jaankaree di or pakistan ke is daawey ko khaarij kar diya ki maamle main or adhik vakt maangane ke unke anurodh ko naamanzoor kar diya gaya he
 Foreign Ministry spokesman Gopal Bagle said that the court has asked Pakistan to complete its arguments by 13 December
 jab baagle se pakistan ke is daawey ke bare main poocha gaya ki bharat ke or adhik vakt dene ke anurodh ko isije ne khaarij kar diya he, to unhone kaha ki yah sach nahin he, kyonki bharat ne chaar maheene maange the or adaalat dwaara sitambar kii samaysima tay kiye jane saath use yah samay mil gaya he
 Earlier, Pakistan's Attorney General Ashtar Ausf Ali was quoted by Dawn News as saying that India had asked the ICJ to give it time till December to present arguments in the Jadhav case, although the court rejected their request
 baagle ne kaha, 'bharat ne yah rukh apanaaya tha ki maamla kisi ke jivan or mrityu kaa he, lekin pakistan ne kaha tha ki isije apil karne ke liye adaalat nahin he
 The ICJ is expected to come up with the result of whether Jadhav can get a counselor or not, for which a period of two to three months is sufficient for filing the reply '
 unhone kaha ki isije ke peethasin adhikari roni abraham kii donon deshon ke pratinidhiyon ke saath aath june ko hui baithkon main samaysima tay kii gai thi
 When Bagle was asked if the hearing in the case would begin after the arguments of the two countries were complete, he said that the court would decide whether it needed more arguments and would then decide on further action
 maamle kii gat 18 may ko sunwaayee ke dauraan isije kii 10 sadasyeey peeth ne pakistan ko jadhav ko faansee dene se roak diya tha
 Jadhav, 46, is a retired Indian Navy officer who was sentenced to death by a Pakistan military court in a case of alleged involvement in espionage and terrorist activities in Pakistan
 maut kii sajaa ke khilaaf bharat aath may ko isije pahunchaa or jadhav ke khilaaf aaropon ko managasaint or unki sunwaayee ko haasyaaspad qaraar diya tha
 The comments (input bhashaa se)(is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) The Foreign Ministry gave this information on Friday and rejected Pakistan's claim that their request for more time in the case has been rejected
 videsh mantralay ke pravaktaa gopal baagle ne bataaya ki adaalat ne pakistan se kaha he ki vah apni daleel 13 disambar tak puri kar le
 When Bagle was asked about Pakistan's claim that India's request for more time has been rejected by the ICJ, he said that this was not true, as India had asked for four months and the court had given the September He has got this time with the deadline set
 isse pehle pakistan ke atorni general ashtar ausaf ali ke hawaale se don news ne kaha ki bharat ne isije se kaha tha ki use jadhav maamle main daleelein dene ke liye disambar tak kaa vakt diya jaae, haalanki adaalat ne unke anurodh ko khaarij kar diya he
 Bagle said, "india had taken the stand that the matter is someone's life and death, but Pakistan had said that the ICJ is not a court to appeal
 isije se is bare main parinaam aane kii apeksha he ki jadhav ko counsal sampark mil saktaa he yaa nahin, jiske liye jawaab daakhil karne ke lihaaj se do se teen maheene kii avadhi kaaphi he'
 He said the deadline was set for the meetings of ICJ presiding officer Ronny Abraham on June 8 with representatives of both countries
 jab baagle se poocha gaya ki kya donon deshon kii daleelein puri hone ke baad maamle main sunwaayee shuru hogi to unhone kaha ki adaalat tay karegi ki use or adhik daleelon kii jarurat he yaa nahin or phir aage kii karrwai par faisla karegi
 During the hearing of the case on May 18, a 10-member bench of the ICJ barred Pakistan from executing Jadhav
 46 varshiya jadhav bhartiya nausena ke sevanivruth adhikari hai, jinhen pakistan kii ek sainya adaalat ne pakistan main jasusi evam aatankwaadi gatividhiyon main kathith sanliptata ke maamle main maut kii sajaa sunai thi
 India reached the ICJ against the death penalty on May 8, calling the allegations against Jadhav concocted and his hearing ridiculous

 ) If children are left inside a hot car for a very short time, then their brain can be seriously damaged or they can even die
 ek shodh ke mutabik baahar kaa taapmaana agar 29 degree celsius he tab shishe chadhe hone kii surat main 10 minute ke bheetar uske andar kaa taapmaana 44 degree celsius tak pahunch saktaa he
 After an interval of 20 minutes, the temperature can reach a very dangerous level of 60 degrees
 tippaniyan Researcher Peter o Miera of La Tobe University said, "children or pets may die or their brain may be severely damaged when locked inside a car
 bacchon ke sharir main bahut jaldi pani kii kami ho jaati he
 This can make them unconscious and they can never be fully healthy again
 " In the last 12 months, around 1500 children have been rescued from inside closed cars
 o miera ke mutabik saamaanya taapmaana kii sthiti main bhi car ke andar band hone par bacchon ko akele band karne kaa asar ghaatak ho saktaa he
 According to a research, if the outside temperature is 29 ° C, then the temperature inside the glass can reach 44 ° c within 10 minutes
 20 minute ke antaraal ke baad to taapmaana 60 degree ke behad khatarnaak str tak pahunch saktaa he
 The comments laa tobe vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakarta peter o miera ne kaha, "car ke andar band hone par bachche yaa phir paaltu jaanavar mar sakate hai yaa phir unka mastishk buree tarah kshatigrast ho saktaa he
 There is a shortage of water in the body of children very quickly
 isse ve behosh ho sakate hai or ve phir kabhi puri tarah swasth nahin ho sakate
 " beete 12 maheenon main kareeb 1500 bacchon ko band kaaron ke andar se bachaaya gaya he
 According to o Miera, the shutdown of children alone can have the effect of shutting down inside the car even under normal temperature conditions
 laa tobe vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakarta peter o miera ne kaha, "car ke andar band hone par bachche yaa phir paaltu jaanavar mar sakate hai yaa phir unka mastishk buree tarah kshatigrast ho saktaa he

 vahiin nigam prati bandar hajaar rupee kharch karata he
